Liam Neeson:Star Wars was the strangest filming experience of my life at the time
In the same GQ interview, actor Liam Neeson said that he saw a lot of strange things on the set of The Phantom Menace that he had never seen before in his acting career.
You know, when we were filming the lightsaber duels, there were a lot of cameras around with a bunch of wires that went to laptops, and there were people sitting at those laptops, working hard. It was the first time I'd seen that in my life. Also, my and Ewan's (Obi-Wan's) lightsabers were wrapped in green ribbons, which were then added to the glow in real time. At first, we made the sounds of turning them on and off ourselves, but George Lucas said it wasn't necessary, as they would add them during the editing process (laughs). - the actor shared.
Nison also said that George Lucas didn't particularly like directing. He enjoyed the final stage, when all his ideas come to life, but Lucas specifically disliked the beginning of the work and the multiple takes.

Star Wars Outlaws fans have launched a petition calling on Ubisoft to develop a sequel to the game
Recently, Ubisoft canceled the development of a sequel to the acclaimed Star Wars Outlaws game due to poor sales and negative reviews. However, many players believe that the game has potential, and they have launched a petition in an attempt to influence the publisher's decision.

Spoiler about the Pope!
It's all by design. It's no coincidence that Lucas scoured dozens of wise books on the eve of the launch of the saga.
So, it's no surprise that the names of the characters in "Star Wars" have a tangible background.
For example, Vader is the Dutch word for "father."
Later, Vader was given the English name Anakin/Anakin, which means "kind and merciful"

Gina Carano and Disney have officially settled their legal dispute
“The Walt Disney Company and Lucasfilm are pleased to announce that they have reached an agreement with Gina Carano regarding her lawsuit against the companies.
Ms. Carano has always been respected by directors, fellow cast members, and the crew, and has put in a lot of effort to improve her skills while being kind and respectful to others.
Now that the legal process is over, we are optimistic about the possibility of working with Ms. Carano in the near future.”
A Lucasfilm spokesperson said in a statement provided to Variety

William Shakespeare's "Mandalorian" has been announced, a retelling of the series' plot in the Shakespearean style from writer Jan Dosher.
Earlier, the plot of all nine episodes of the franchise was retold in the style of Shakespeare's plays. The idea came to Dasher after he read Seth Grahame-Smith's novel Pride, Prejudice and Zombies, rewatched the original Star Wars trilogy, and visited the Oregon Shakespeare Festival.
The series is not canonical within the Star Wars universe and is a creative interpretation of the events in the films.

Yesterday, the D23 Expo panel was held, where Disney made several announcements about their franchises
🤨
Behind closed doors, they showed materials from the Mandalorian and Grogu movie, the same ones that were shown to the selected ones (people with a VIP ticket) at Star Wars Celebration 2025. Nothing new. But the strangest thing is that they didn't put these materials in the public domain again, despite the fact that they were leaked a long time ago.
The film "The Mandalorian and Grogu" is scheduled for release in May 2026, but its advertising campaign is perhaps the most terrible in the history of Star Wars. LucasFilm seems to have completely forgotten about it. Ironically, the first promotional materials for the film "Starfighter" were released earlier, even though its premiere is scheduled for a year later. I don't know how to comment on this. They will once again complain about poor box office performance and blame everyone but themselves.

Natalie Portman (Padmé Amidala) suffered because of her role in Star Wars
😱
As we know, not all actors in Star Wars spoke warmly about their roles in the film saga. For example, Alec Guinness (Obi-Wan from OT) and Harrison Ford (Han Solo) openly said that they did not like their characters, and George Lucas even had to persuade them to continue working. But actress Natalie Portman also complained about her role.
According to the actress, her career suffered greatly after her role as Padmé Amidala in the prequel trilogy. After the high-profile premiere of the films, Portman found herself on the "blacklist" of influential directors. No one wanted to cast her in the lead role in a "Star Wars: Padmé" movie. Natalie had to put in a lot of effort and gain the support of major Hollywood bosses to break the association between her and Senator Amidala, and to get producers to cast her in major roles again.
In any case, the actress remembers her work on Star Wars with warmth.

The development of the Star Wars
#Eclipse
game is still ongoing.
The Art of The High Republic: Volume II guidebook released on August 19 confirmed that the game is still in active development and will be released in the next couple of years. The production is still being handled by the
#QuanticDream
studio.
According to the developers, Eclipse will have a new combat system and will not be similar to the studio's previous games.

#Skywalker

#Mandalorian

#Jedi

#Luke
as a master Jedi, even though he was the most idealistic hero, the one who always rose from the blows of fate and responded to defeats. When the opportunity came up to show it, I thought, ‘Damn, this is great!’” Mark said in a new interview with
#THR

Let me remind you that the next Star Wars game will be Star Wars Zero Company
🎮
Players will experience a single-player turn-based tactical strategy in the XCOM universe. The project is being developed by Bit Reactor, Respawn Entertainment, and Lucasfilm Games. It is expected to be released on PlayStation 5, Xbox Series X|S, and PC in 2026. More specifically, the game is being developed by the creators of the Cal Kestis and XCOM games.
The action takes place at the end of the Clone Wars. Players will take on the role of Hawks, a former Republic officer who commands the Zero Company, an extraordinary group of professional mercenaries from across the galaxy.
Although the project may seem secondary and entertaining due to its style, the developers promise a complex and cinematic storyline that will become part of the new Star Wars canon.

Actor Timothy Olyphant (Cobb Vance) doesn't know anything about his character's future in Star Wars.
🤔
Last week, the actor spoke with the author of the RingerVerse channel and revealed that he has no idea what awaits Cobb Vance after "The Book of Boba Fett." According to Olyphant, he has been in contact with Favreau and Filoni to clarify this matter, but has not received a response.
Cobb Vance is one of the secondary characters in The Mandalorian, who has become a favorite among viewers. The ending of The Book of Boba Fett hinted at his future, but this hint has yet to be developed.

Early developments of the Star Wars: Knights of the Old Republic remake by the Aspyr studio have surfaced
😱
In the portfolio of the former artist, they found developments for the initial level and an early prototype with a modular weapon system. The developments date back to 2020. Apparently, the screenshots were taken at the very early stage of development. Later, the Aspyr studio was removed from the project and it was handed over to Saber Interactive.
According to Saber's creative director, Tim Willits, the remake is still in progress and has not been canceled.

🔥
ILM has unveiled a new project, Star Wars: Beyond Victory!
🤖
Industrial Light & Magic has announced a mixed reality (MR) project called Star Wars: Beyond Victory, which will be released on October 7, 2025, exclusively for Meta Quest 3 and 3S.
In this project, players will be able to engage in iconic battles from the Star Wars galaxy, control ships, use the Force, and interact with their surroundings using augmented reality technologies.
According to the first footage, Beyond Victory offers a unique experience where your room becomes a battlefield and droids, Sith, and Jedi appear nearby
🗡
This is ILM's first Star Wars project in MR format, created specifically for Meta Quest 3.

This is a great project: actress
#MiaGoth
has revealed details about the new Star Wars: Starfighter movie
🔔
The character that Mia Goth will play has not yet been revealed, but according to rumors, she has been cast as an antagonist. However, the actress has shared her thoughts on working on the new Star Wars movie and provided some hints about the plot.
"It's really challenging, but I love it. I'm being asked to do things that I haven't done before on set. This is a separate film, not a prequel, an independent story with new characters. There's a wonderful script here, really good text. There is a lot of soul, adventure and original characters in this scenario. Levy is the perfect director for this story," said Mia Goth.
Filming is currently underway. Right now, director Sean Levy is using actors Ryan Gosling, Matt Smith, Amy Adams, Mia Goth and Flynn Gray in the expanses of the Mediterranean Sea.
The
#Starfighter
premiere is scheduled for May 28, 2027

Disney has revealed the exact budget of the film "
Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker
" - it's incredibly huge
💼
According to new data, the ninth episode of Star Wars cost
#LucasFilm
and Disney a whopping $593 million. This is double the amount announced by the company at the time of filming ($275 million). The high budget includes production, marketing, and unforeseen expenses. As a result, "
Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker
is one of the leaders in the "most expensive film in history" category.
This proves once again that for a film of this scale to pay off, it is necessary to collect at least two or even three of its budgets at the box office.
"
Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker
was able to pay off, earning $1.1 billion in theaters.
🤧
P.S. We remind you that the budget of the series "Obi-Wan Kenobi" is only $90 million.

George Lucas has admitted that he is no longer interested in Star Wars
🤔
In a new interview with The Wall Street Journal, the legendary director said that he does not follow the development of his franchise.
"Now Star Wars is in the hands of Disney and they are implementing their ideas. I have long since moved away from this. Now I am busy with my own life and building a museum, and by the way, it is more difficult than making a movie," Lucas said.
George Lucas is currently focused on creating his own Museum of Narrative Art, which is set to open in 2026. He also remains one of Disney's largest shareholders and continues to receive significant commissions from all modern Star Wars revenue.

Adam Driver said that he worked on a new Star Wars movie called "The Hunt for Ben Solo" with director Steven Soderbergh.
• The plot was supposed to unfold after the events of "Skywalker. The Rise."
• Disney liked the idea, but the studio rejected the project because they "didn't understand how Ben Solo could survive."
• Adam Driver called the script for "The Hunt for Ben Solo" "one of the coolest damn scripts he's ever been involved in."
• The actor says that the canceled film "The Hunt for Ben Solo" was inspired by "The Empire Strikes Back."
Adam Driver on the canceled film "The Hunt for Ben Solo":
"I've always been interested in doing another Star Wars movie. We've been talking about it since 2021. Kathleen Kennedy contacted me. I always said, if there's a great director and a great story, I'll be on board right away. I adored this character and loved playing him," Adam Driver told AP News.

Adam Driver said that he worked on a new Star Wars movie called "The Hunt for Ben Solo" with director Steven Soderbergh.
• The plot was supposed to unfold after the events of "Skywalker. The Rise."
• Disney liked the idea, but the studio rejected the project because they "didn't understand how Ben Solo could survive."
• Adam Driver called the script for "The Hunt for Ben Solo" "one of the coolest damn scripts he's ever been involved in."
• The actor says that the canceled film "The Hunt for Ben Solo" was inspired by "The Empire Strikes Back."
#AdamDriver
on the canceled film "The Hunt for Ben Solo":
"I've always been interested in doing another Star Wars movie. We've been talking about it since 2021. Kathleen Kennedy contacted me. I always said, if there's a great director and a great story, I'll be on board right away. I adored this character and loved playing him," Adam Driver told AP News.

Fans are asking Disney to resume work on the film Star Wars: The Hunt for Ben Solo
😰
The situation has taken an unexpected turn. After Adam Driver revealed the canceled film about the redemption of Ben Solo, the events of which were supposed to take place after the trilogy of Star Wars sequels, many people began to demand that Disney resume work on the project furiously. It got to the point where someone hung a poster with the request "bring back Ben Solo" on a plane and specifically flew near the company's office.
Steven Soderbergh, who was supposed to be the director of the film, joined the discussion. According to him, Disney behaved strangely, since the project had a serious level of development. It was not only the script that was ready: the top of Disney received a fully formed plot, a budget estimate and an approximate date for the start of filming.
However, Disney executives Alan Bergman and Bob Iger refused to approve the film because of the death of Ben Solo
☠️

The
#KnightsofRen
were conceived as a "workaround" to the Rule of Two.
Since this ancient Sith law prohibited more than two Sith from existing at the same time (master and apprentice), the idea was that a Sith stranger would become the founder of a cult associated with the Sith but not technically Sith.
Thus, the Rule of Two is maintained, as
#Plagis
has an apprentice in
#Palpatine
, and there are no other Sith. But at the same time, through the Knights of Ren, the Sith continue their influence, creating an external group of followers of the Dark Side who operate outside of strict
#Sith
rules.
According to showrunner Leslie Headland, as outlined in The Art of The
#Acolyte

The Final Star Destroyer
The Terminator is one of the most formidable warships of the First Order era, a Resurgent‑class star destroyer.
Its armament included more than 1,500 turbolasers and ion cannons, point protection turrets, rocket launchers and tractor beam projectors. The powerful propulsion system—eight Gemon‑8 ion engines and three destroyer engines—provided excellent maneuverability, while the first-class hyperdrive allowed the ship to move quickly between systems. The air wing consisted of TIE/fo, TIE/sf, and TIE/se fighters and bombers.
The Executor was formally considered Kylo Ren's personal flagship, although General Hux and Captain Edrison Pivi were more often in charge of operational control. This ship became not just a combat unit, but a mobile decision-making center and a symbol of the First Order's strict vertical of power.

#RUMOR
:
#LucasFilm
plans to show the original 1977 version of A New Hope in theaters!
The company has already announced a re-release of Star Wars: A New Hope in 2027 to celebrate the 50th anniversary. However, according to some insiders, LucasFilm is working on restoring the very first version of the film, without the special effects and additional scenes that were added to the 2006 Special Edition.
This is done to give fans the opportunity to see Star Wars as George Lucas envisioned it back in the 70s. LucasFilm will restore the image, but preserve the original vision.

#Acolyte
Against the backdrop of the fans' campaign for the release of the cancelled film "The Hunt for Ben Solo", actor Manny Jacinto shared his thoughts on the possible continuation of "Acolyte":

head Kathleen Kennedy called "The Hunt for

" the first film in her memory that Disney did not approve with a finished script.
Her words were conveyed by director Steven Soderbergh for
#TheWrap
, who was involved in the project with Adam Driver. Sources also revealed new details:
• The original version of the script belonged to Rebecca Blunt, who worked with Soderbergh on "Logan Lucky."
• Scott Z. Burns (Contagion, The Bourne Ultimatum) was paid more than any other writer in Lucasfilm history to complete the script.
• Kathleen Kennedy, Dave Filoni, and Carrie Beck were directly involved in the development process.
• The plot was supposed to revive Ben Solo, and his location would have been the main intrigue.
• The film had a final script, a budget, and was ready to start filming before they submitted it to Disney and were rejected.

Kanan Jarrus, born Caleb Dum, is a Jedi who survived
#Order66
.
As a Padawan during the Clone Wars, he narrowly escaped extermination and spent years hiding his connection to the Force, working as a smuggler and mercenary under an assumed name.
His life changed when he met the crew of the Ghost, who became his family. Kanan reclaimed his Jedi identity and took on the apprenticeship of a Force-sensitive orphan, Ezra Bridger. He became the leader of a small rebel cell, which later expanded into the broader Rebel Alliance.
Kanan Jarrus is known for his heroic act of self-sacrifice, where he gave his life to save his friends from an explosion, proving that the true power of a Jedi lies in their love and willingness to protect those they hold dear. He left behind a legacy as a mentor who revived the Jedi tradition during the dark times of the Empire.

#interesting
The Mechanism of Chewbacca's Costume
Two departments worked on the materialization of Chewbacca. The costumers sewed, and under the leadership of Stewart, a mask-head was created.
In the mask, Freeborn used the same mechanism as in "2001: A Space Odyssey" for apes. The rigid polyurethane skull fit the actor perfectly, including a hinged jaw.
When the actor opened his mouth, not only did his jaw move, but his skin also stretched, mimicking the behavior of real skin.
The plastic, thin skin was first painted, and then long strands were individually attached using a hypodermic needle.
Inside, the mask was equipped with a system of toggle switches and plates that the actor could manipulate with his tongue, causing
#Chewbacca
's lips to move.

Sam Witwer is confident that fans will be pleased with the new animated series "Maul: The Shadow Lord":
"I really like this series. And I'm not just saying that - I've watched it in its entirety, in different versions. It's a cool project, and it's very different from anything we've done before," the actor said during Rebel Scum Con.
1. The series will show how Maul is processing the changes in the Galaxy - after all, he himself was once at the origins of the Palpatine Empire.
2. Maul misses the Jedi, as the fall of the Order took away the magic, colors, and chivalry that he grew up with. Now it's all dead.
3. Maul won't become a hero, but he will fiercely oppose the Empire. Whitwer describes him as an "8.5 out of 10 villain" - not a saint, but not as monstrous as Emperor Palpatine or Vader.
4. Maul is ready to pass on his accumulated wisdom to a new apprentice.
5.
#Maul
will undergo a serious internal transformation and change as a character, but he will remain a dangerous and powerful force user.

The
#Superlaser
of the Second
#DeathStar
After the destruction of the first Death Star, the
#Emperor
immediately began construction of a second one. It had several notable improvements that not only fixed design flaws, but also improved the main superlaser.
This laser could cool down and recharge for the next shot in just a few minutes, rather than hours, which was a significant improvement. It could also narrow its beam and track much smaller targets, such as large ships, making it a versatile combat station rather than a specialized planetary destroyer.

The official Star Wars
#Insider
magazine will cease to exist in 2026
😔
The magazine has existed under various names since 1978, and under its current name since 1994. It has featured exclusive news, articles, and stories about our beloved universe, all published by LucasFilm's own publishing house. Occasionally, it has even provided interesting details about upcoming premieres.
The final issues will be dedicated to the 10th anniversary of The Force Awakens and Rogue One. It is likely that LucasFilm wants to replace the personal publishing with a collaboration with Empire or Vanity Fair

<sub>👁 318 · [05:45 · 13 Nov 2025](https://t.me/INSTARWARS/4830)</sub>

Obi-Wan's message in
#FallenOrder
is taken directly from the Star Wars: Rebels series.
Those who have played Fallen Order will understand that the Holocrons were used to store information, but they may have forgotten that Obi-Wan
#Kenobi
left a message after investigating the massacre at the Jedi Temple, warning other Jedi to go into hiding, and that this was also stored in a Holocron. The said message is played in Fallen Order, but it is actually a reference to both Episode III and Star Wars:
#Rebels
.
James Arnold Taylor is once again reprising his role as Obi-Wan after voicing him in both Clone Wars and Rebels, and these sounds are an exact re-enactment of what we saw in the series.

About
#lightsabers
🗡
An important element is the kyber crystal, which focuses energy and the
#Force
.
🗡
Crystals determine the color of the blade, symbolizing the personal characteristics of the Jedi. For example, the purple sword of Master Windu symbolizes his proximity to the dark side.
🗡
Red Sith
#lightsabers
are created artificially, being saturated with dark energy, while the Jedi use natural crystals.

It looks like we have a SCANDAL on our hands.
Lucasfilm/Disney has been accused of copying the choreography of a 2019 fan film for one of the episodes of "The Vision."
The accusations were made by the director of the independent fan film "Dark Jedi," which was released in 2019. He posted a viral video on the network with a comparison, where the frames from his work are clearly compared to the key moments of the duel from the 7th episode of the 2nd season of "Visions".
And the videos are really similar.
This episode of "Visions" was created by the Indian animation studio 88 Pictures. Disney and Lucasfilm have not commented on the situation.
What do you think?

Sabine Wren was never originally planned to be a Jedi during the making of Rebels, executive producer Henry Gilroy said.
“That was absolutely not part of the plan… We felt that not only would it interfere with Ezra’s story, but it would also be a repeat of what had already happened.
The idea of Sabine training as a Jedi when she was already an exceptional warrior on her own path seemed like an overkill to us,” Gilroy says on the Pod of Rebellion podcast

The new Bailan Skoll was originally supposed to be Andor's friend
😱
It has long been known that in the 2nd season of
#Ahsoka
we will be introduced to the new Bailan Skoll, played by actor Rory McCann, who will replace the deceased Ray Stevenson. But do you know why else they took McCann for the role? Recently, a very funny and at the same time sad story came to light. Before joining the film universe, the actor could appear in another project - in
#Andor
. More precisely, he already starred in it.
He was originally cast as Brasso, the protagonist's best friend, but circumstances intervened. Shortly after filming began, McCann suffered a serious injury, and doctors strongly recommended surgery. The actor was forced to interrupt filming and undergo rehabilitation. The doctor bluntly stated, "If you don't have surgery, you'll lose the ability to walk."
Ultimately, Rory was removed from the project, and his role was recast with actor Chuk Sibeay.

<sub>👁 368 · [19:48 · 02 Dec 2025](https://t.me/INSTARWARS/4905)</sub>

#Mandalorian
and
#Grogu
":
"The Galactic
#Empire
has been defeated, and its remnants are scattered across the galaxy. However, some former Dark Age commanders continue to cling to power and have become dangerous warlords. Din Djarin and his apprentice, Grogu, track down and neutralize these pockets of resistance.

The Old Republic is officially returning to the canon — Lucasfilm has announced Star Wars: Fate of The Old Republic, marking the long-awaited revival of one of the franchise's most beloved eras.
The project is led by Casey Hudson, the legendary creative director of the original KOTOR and the Mass Effect trilogy, a man who was at the forefront of modern role-playing space operas.
His return to the Star Wars universe is an event in itself: he helped shape the Old Republic, and now he gets to reimagine it for a new generation of fans.

The developers emphasize that the Fate of The Old Republic game is not a remake or a direct adaptation of the Revan/Malak story, but rather an independent canonical project that aims to redefine the era of "The Old Republic" in the modern timeline.
The authors describe the game as a "blank canvas," offering a space for new and original stories while maintaining a deep respect for the spirit and aesthetics of classic Star Wars.
The game is currently in the early stages of production, and it is too early to discuss a release date.

Harrison Ford will be honored with the Screen Actors Guild (SAG-AFTRA) Lifetime Achievement Award.
The legendary actor, at the age of 83, will become the 61st recipient of the SAG-AFTRA Lifetime Achievement Award, the highest recognition the Guild bestows for an outstanding career, long-term impact on the industry and humanitarian work.
The gala ceremony will take place on March 1, 2026, marking another symbolic milestone in the career of one of the world’s leading film icons.

⚡️
Kathleen Kennedy on
The Last Jedi
and Rian Johnson, years later
Nine years after the release of Episode 8, Kathleen Kennedy has once again spoken about the film and its director, Rian Johnson.
According to her, she still considers the movie one of the best in the entire
Star Wars
saga.
At the same time, Kennedy noted that the negative reaction from part of the audience had a significant impact on Johnson. In her view, the director was “scared” by the scale of the criticism, and this was one of the reasons why he did not continue working on new
Star Wars
films.
Kennedy emphasized that such a reaction from fans creates a difficult atmosphere around the franchise: many directors and actors, when joining
Star Wars
, fear the consequences and wonder in advance what kind of reaction they will have to face.
